# summary TLSW gives same output

    Code
      summary(x.TLSW)
    Output
      Spectral estimation was performed:
      -smoothing was performed using mean smoothing with binwidth 45.
      -maximum wavelet scale analysed is scale 6.
      -boundary handling was used.
      -----------

      -estimation was performed using a decimated wavelet transform with linear thresholding.
      -maximum wavelet scale analysed is scale 6.
      -boundary handling was used.
